Lets drive into the air!\r\n\r\nA hovercraft, also known as an air-cushion vehicle or ACV, is a craft capable of travelling over land, water, mud or ice and other surfaces. Hovercraft are hybrid vessels operated by a pilot as an aircraft.\r\n\r\nHovercraft use blowers to produce a large volume of air below the hull that is slightly above atmospheric pressure. The pressure difference between the higher pressure air below the hull and lower pressure ambient air above it produces lift, which causes the hull to float above the running surface. For stability reasons, the air is typically blown through slots or holes around the outside of a disk- or oval-shaped platform, giving most \r\nhovercraft a characteristic rounded-rectangle shape. Typically this cushion is contained within a flexible \"skirt\", which allows the vehicle to travel over small obstructions without damage.\r\n\r\nEnjoy fast-paced action in our Hovercraft Simulator.
